 loktantr main prayukt 'lok' shabd apane apaar vistaar main samast sankeernataaon se mukt he
 'lok' is a joint inclusive unit of the group like caste, religion, language, region-class, in which the liberal sense of coexistence actively gives the basis to 'lok'
 'lok' main sabake prati sabaki sahanubhuti kaa hona aavashyak he
 From this, 'lok' gets organized as a unit and earns its vitality
 'jio or jeene do' kaa udaar vichaar lok-sangrah kaa maargdarshi siddhant he or is siddhant par aadhaarit 'lok' main nyaay, samanta or shanti kii pratishtha ke liye 'lok' ne swashasit 'tantra' ke rup main loktantr ko samast shashan tantron main shreshth maanya kiya he
 With the attainment of independence, India accepted the democratic system
 hamaare samvidhan ke prarambh main prastut pankti 'ham bharat ke log
 
 
 'witness our inclusive nature
 is 'ham' main 'sarv' kaa bhav he- kisi varg, varna, sampradaay, samooh, aadi kaa nahin
 The word 'we' indicates 'survey Bhavantu Sukhinah'
 is 'ham' main samast bharatvasiyon ke kalyaan or utthan kii udaar bhaavana samahit he
 'sabka Saath, Sabka Vikas' is its determination and in the fulfillment of this resolution, our freedom and autonomy have meaning
 samasamyik sandarbh main is satya ko eemaandaaree se sweekaar karne kii aavashyaktaa he- 'lok' (jansamanya) ko bhi or 'tantra' (netritv-prashasan) ko bhi
 It is conceivable that our 'tantra', constantly repeating the pledge of commitment to the unity and integrity of the country at the theoretical level and raising public breathtaking slogans of social-justice, equality and harmony, in the hope of gaining unrestricted authority over power on the practical plane
 Today, our democracy is plagued with terrible problems due to the codenamed creations of 'lok' divided into several groups to form banks
 bhadakaau bhaashan, samast 'lok' ke sthaan par 'samooh vishesh' ke hitsaadhan kaa praytn, ugr-hinsak andolan or aankadon ke ganit main uljhi kathith raajnneeti ne janajivan ko asantosh, ashaanti asuraksha or bhay se bhar diya he
 The autocracy of 'lok' and the dictatorship of 'tantra' are treading the path of freedom
 ek ore 'lok' tathakthith andolanon ke bahaane hinsa par utaaru he, vaahan phunke ja rahe hai, nirdosho kii hatya ho rahi he, sadakon par doodh bahaya ja rahaa he, subjiyan phenki ja rahi hai, saarvajanik jivan ashaant kiya ja rahaa he-- arthath vah sab ho rahaa he jo loktantr main 'lok' (janata) ko nahin karnaa chahie
 On the other hand, 'tantra' is seen lashing sticks and bullets at the fiercest agitators, sometimes accepting their just and unreasonable demands, distributing compensation and kneeling
 donon hi sthitiyaan loktantr ke swasthya ke liye hanikaarak hai
 Our current aforementioned position is responsible for the power greed of the system, the tendency to appease a group or class to get power and the corrupt politics of caste-religion based vote bank
 loktantr main satta janata kii seva kaa madhyam he, vilasitapurna saamanti durbhilaashaaon kii purti kaa nahin
 There is no struggle on the path of service, but the desire to accumulate more and more amenities, the desire to collect personal luxuries on the strength of the people's hard-earned money, creates fierce competition among political parties
 durbhaagya se hamaara loktantr isi disha main agrasar he
 It has become a priority today to move the chariot of power from the turbulent path of luxury to the path of service and sacrifice
 aaj saarvajanik raajnneetik jivan main vaaksanyam atyaavashyak ho gaya he kyonki bade padon par baithe logon dwaara kahi gai baaten jansadharan ke kriya-path kaa vinishchay karti hai
 The lack of speech in our leadership is having a negative effect on our society
 kadaachit bhartiya raajnneeti main swatantraaa prapti ke tatkaal pashchaat se hi yah dosha se vyaapt ho gaya tha
 That is why the famous poet Pandit Shyamnarayan Pandey warned in the epic 'shivaji' published in 1956 - Do not let frantic speeches deceive Khor Netadesh
 anurakt anushaasit praja kijindagi dahakaa na den 
 
 lagbhag saath varsh purv mahakavi ne hamen jo chetavanee di thi uske prati asaavadhaanee darshane kaa dushprinaam aaj hamaare saamne he
 The current socio-political conditions testify to this fact
 durbhaagya se aaj 'lok' vibhinn raajnneetik dalon main banta hua he
 Every ordinary citizen is directly or indirectly close to some party at the level of thought and fully believes in his or her leader's point - whether it is true or not
 yah sthiti chintajanak he
 It is natural to trust the leader of your choice but it is not in the interest of democracy to blindly support his wrong decisions
 ise kisi bhi sthiti main uchit nahin kaha ja saktaa
 Normally, 'lok' moves on the path guided by its 'tantra' but in the present adversity, 'lok' needs to move forward and guide the 'tantra'
 voton ke chunavi ganit main uljhi tushtikaran kii aatmghaatee raajnneeti karne waalon ke kaaran 'tantra' apane 'lok' ko sahi disha nahin de paa rahaa he
 Therefore, the 'lok' has to create his own path of welfare on the principle of 'app Deepo Bhava'
 daleey dal-dal main dhanse samoohon ke hit kii raajnneeti karne waalon ko sahi disha dikhaani hogi or yah tab sambhav hoga jab 'lok' samooh vishesh ke hit-saadhan kii sankeern maansikta se ubarkar, nijee swaarthon kii bali dekar sampurna samaaj ke liye samarpit sevabhaav se kaary karne vaale samajaseviyon ko tantra main pratishthit kare, aparaadhik prishthbhumi vaale bahubaliyon ko tantra main pravesh na karne de
 It is only with such activation of 'lok' that improvement in 'tantra' will be possible and our democracy will be able to continue its development journey
 loktantr ko bheed-tantra main badalanaa khatarnaak khel he
 'tantra' has been openly playing this game in the form of rallies, meetings, visits
 shakti-pradarshan kii is hode main shakti, samay or dhan kaa durupyog to hota hi he, saath hi janajivan bhi yatayaat aadi vyavasthaaon ke baadhit hone se asuvidha anubhav karata he
 The same mob, by becoming violent and violent, also damages national property
 apriy ghatnaayen ghatati hai
 Today, when the government has many effective resources like Doordarshan, newspapers, email, social media available to reach the people and the people to the government, what is the rationale of such crowded demonstrations and meetings? For the protection of national property in the public interest, both 'lok' and 'tantra' need to avoid mobilization
 loktantr main prayek naagarik kii bhoomika ek jaagruk prahari kii hoti he
 With the awareness of 'public', 'tantra' cannot take wrong decisions, it cannot do its own arbitrary and conscious 'tantra' does not allow criminal elements to flourish in public welfare
 is prakaar loktantr kii safalataa 'lok' or 'tantra' donon kii jaagrukta par nirbhar karti he
 The irony is that today we express awareness about our collective interests, not the public interest
 yadi ham vibhajit maansikta ko tyagkar rashtriya-chetana ke ek sutara main bandha kar saare samaaj ke hit-sadhano ke liye jaagruk hon, aapasi vaimnasy bhoolen, vigat ghatnaon kii katutaa tyagkar parsparik sahyog kaa sankalp len to hamaara loktantr adhik shashakt or sarthak banegaa
 It is worth remembering that the vitality of our democracy is in coordination between different groups, not in conflict

 There is no connection with the illegal colony bill from Delhi elections - purikejriwal government asked for time till 2021: Union Urban Development Minister Hardeep Singh Puri on Monday participated in the Agenda Aaj Tak 2019 flight session
 puri ne centre sarkaar kii yojanaon ke saath hi avaidh coloniyon se jude bill par bhi khulkar baat kii
 Puri rejected Chief Minister Arvind Kejriwal's claims about illegal colonies in Delhi and challenged him to come and speak on a public platform
 dilli vidhansabha chunaav se pahaleavaidh colonionko regularise karne ke bill ko lekar puche gaye sawaal ke jawaab main puri ne kaha ki in 1731 coloniyon main 40 se 50 lakh log rahete hai
 In 2008, when Sheila Dixit was the Chief Minister in Delhi, she had decided that the people of these colonies should get ownership and facilities
 centre kii manmohan singh sarkaar ne kaha tha ki iske liye dilli sarkaar jimmedaar he
 He said that it has nothing to do with the Delhi elections
 mukhyamantri arvind kejariwal or unki aam aadmi party (aap) kii ore se yah nirnay dilli sarkaar ke dabaav main liye jane ke daavon ko khaarij karte hue puri ne unhenpublic plateformpar aakar baat karne kii chunauti di
 He said that Kejriwal first accused the people and then apologized
 puri ne kaha ki jab mantralay main kaarybhaar sambhala or avaidh coloniyon ke sambandh main jaankaree lee to pataa chalaa ki dilli sarkaar ne digital masping karaane kii baat karte hue do saal kaa samay maanga he

 On the occasion of the launch of 'uvcan', an initiative of the Yuvraj Singh Foundation to combat cancer, Yuvraj said, "it is a matter of pride that BCCI has sent my name for the Arjuna Award
" ummid he ki is baar mujhe yah puraskaar mil jayega
 There was a misunderstanding between the BCCI and the Sports Ministry over the last date for Arjuna Award nomination
 bisisiai ne aarope lagaaya tha ki unhen pehle kii tarah namakan ke bare main suchit nahin kiya gaya tha
 This was denied by the Sports Ministry
 kuch din pehle haalanki khel mantralay ke sanyukt sachiv mukul chatarji ne bisisiai ko suchit kiya ki namakan kii avadhi 20 july tak badha di gai he
 If he was awarded the country's highest sporting honor, established in 1991–92, he would become the third cricketer to receive the award after Sachin Tendulkar (1997–98) and Mahendra Singh Dhoni (2007–08)

 haalanki film ke nirdeshak farhaan akhtar kaa is par riection aayaa tha or unhone film kaa sikval banane se manaa kar diya tha

 akshay ne apni apakaming film section 375 ke trailor launch par media se ek baatcheet main kaha- ''maine hameshaa se farhaan se ye baat kahi he ki film kaa sikval banane ke liye ve ham teenon ke 50 saal puure hone kaa intazaar karen iske baad ve dil chahta he 2 ko banane ke bare main sochen
 "" Aamir is 50 years old, in some time Saif Ali Khan will also be 50 years old, i will take some time to become 50 years old
 abhi meri umr 44 saal kii he

 us samay or maahaul ke hisaab se ye film banaai gai thi
 At that time i also wanted to make this film
 magar ab aisa ho paanaa mushkil he
 Talking about Akshaye Khanna's film article 375, the film is directed by Ajay Bahl
 film ke bare main baat karte hue akshay khanna ne kaha- maine ye film isliye kii kyonki main ajay kii riting se puri tarah se prabhavit rahaa hum

 film kii kahani paripakv he or isamen kaaphi gaharaai he

 film agle maheene 13 sitambar ko relies kii jaaegi
 a doctor in Patan, Gujarat left the bandage in the patient's body after the operation
 jurmaane ke taur par ab unhen aath lakh rupee marij ko dene honge
 The insurance company was also convicted in the case which insured the hospital
 lihaaja ab puure 12 saal tak 9 fisadi byaaj dar par insurance company ko paise chukaane honge
 Apart from this, the patient will have to pay 10 thousand rupees in lieu of the problems and expenses he faced in the court-court
 mamala 2002 kaa he jab gayanacologist dow
 Vandana Amin operated Uteras of Meetaben Patel, a resident of Surat
 surgery ke badakapade kaa ek tukdaa marij ke sharir menhi rah gaya
 Then the victim had to undergo an operation at another place and then the garbage could be removed from her body
 lekin tab tak uske sharir ko kaaphi nuksaan ho chukaa tha
 In 2003, the woman approached the consumer court and asked for Rs 10 lakh as compensation
 maamle kii sunwaayee puri hone par court ne kaha,'doctor kii laaparvaahise marij kii antadee kharaab ho gai
 Therefore, the doctor will have to pay a fine of Rs 8 lakh to the patient
 ' court ne beemaa company ko bhi maamle main doshi banaaya
 The doctor and insurance company appealed to the Gujarat State Consumer Dispute Redress Commission against the court order
 lekin yahaan bhi faisla marij ke haq main aayaa
 Out of tolerance, the entire havoc of North India is being destroyed by the intense havoc of summer
 andhra pradesh or telugana main aasmaan se aag barasana jari he or deshbhar main ab tak surya ke prakope se 1400 se zyada logon kii maut ho gai he
 Many parts of the country are in the grip of scorching heat
 sabase zyada logon kii mrityu andhra pradesh or telugana rajyon main hui he
 The total number of people who died of heat stroke reached 1412, while the death toll in Andhra Pradesh and Telangana alone reached 1360
 taaja aankadon ke mutabik, andhra pradesh main lu se marane waalon kii sankhya 1020 ho chuki he
 In Telangana, 340 people have been killed due to heat stroke
 telugana main mangalvaar-buudhvaar tak 74 or andhra pradesh main 168 logon kii maut ho chuki he
 Two died in Delhi, meanwhile, there are reports of death of Lu Sedo in the southern part of the national capital
 hyderabad main mausam vibhaag ke nideshak waike reddy ne bataaya ki telugana main agle do din or tateey andhra pradesh main teen din or tej garm hawaaen chalengi
 He said that due to being outside in the heat for a long time, this death can happen
 duusari ore, maidani bhaagon main uttar pradesh main buudhvaar ko agra sabase garm rahaa or yahaan kaa taapmaana 46 degree celsius ko paar kar gaya
 Temperatures in many areas of Haryana and Punjab also remained between 41 and 45 degrees Celsius and hot winds continued to rage in both the states
 andhrapradesh main prakasham jile main sabase zyada kul 202 log lu kii vajah se maare gaye hai
 Besides, 130 people have died in Guntur district, 112 in Visakhapatnam, 78 in Vijayanagar and 74 in Nellore
 reddy ne kaha ki sarkaar ne chikitsakon ko lu se peedit logon ko chikitsiya sahaayta muhaiyaa karaane ke liye sajag rahane ko kaha he
 a senior official of the disaster management department of Telangana state said that Nalgonda district in the state has the highest number of people killed at 99
 iske alaava khammam main 72, karimnagar main 45 or mehboobnagar main 37logon kii mrityuho gai he
 43 people are reported to have died due to heat stroke in Odisha and seven in Gujarat
 -input bhashaa se Legendary boxer Akhil Kumar, who is conferred with the Arjuna Award, says he does not want to stop in life, just keep moving forward and that is why he has stepped into professional boxing
 ioes ne profeshnal boxing ke liye akhil kumaar or bharat ke liye kai antarrashtriya padak jeet chuke jitendra kumaar ke saath shanivaar ko qaraar kiya
 Under this agreement, Akhil and Jeetendra will be seen entering the ring after a long time in a professional boxing competition in Mumbai on April 1
 peshewar lig ke liye mili prerana ke bare main ieenes ke saath saakshaatkaar main akhil ne kaha, "profeshnal boxing main aane kaa koi khaas kaaran nahin he mere paas
 i only want to move forward in life
 ruknaa nahin chahta
 " varsh 2005 main arjuna puraskaar hasil karne vaale mukkebaaz akhil ne kaha, "ham khilaadiyon kii pahchaan hamaare khel se he
 i know people as a boxer and if i sit down for that, then it is no use
 main jivan main kuch na kuch karte rahanaa chahta hum
 " profeshnal boxing main aane ke peeche vijender singh se protsaahan ke bare main akhil ne kaha, "vijender se pehle bhi kai mukkebaaz profeshnal boxing main aae hai, jinamein rajkumaar sangwan, venkatesh, arjuna puraskaar se sammanit dharmedra yadav shaamil hai
 " ullekhneey he ki bharat ko disambar, 2012 main tatkaaleen bhartiya ameor mukkebaaji mahasang (iabf) ke liye chayan main herpher ke maamle main pratibandhit kar diya gaya tha
 Due to this ban, Indian boxers did not get an opportunity to play under the national flag in international competitions
 haalanki, pichley saal antarrashtriya ameor mukkebaaji sangh (iba) ne bhartiya mukkebaaji mahasang (bieggai) ko manyata de di
 In such a scenario, Akhil said, “sports Ministry has helped a lot in the past as well
 khilaadiyon ke liye vah har saal bajet paas karte hai
 " in ghatnaon ke kaaran profeshnal boxing main aane ke sanshay ke bare main akhil ne kaha, "mere profeshnal boxing main kadam rakhane ke peeche mukkebaaji sangh kii kami kaaran nahin he
 The government has helped in every way
 maine olympic khelon, rashtramandal khelon or antarrashtriya pratiyogitaaon kaa anubhav le liya he or ab kuch nayaa karne kaa man he
 That is why i have come to professional boxing
 iskaa pratibandh se koi lenaa-dena nahin he
 " akhil ne kaha ki bieggai jis prakaar se kaary kar rahi he, unhen aashaa he ki bahut hi jald ameor mukkebaaji main achche parinaam bhi dekhne ko milenge
 Apart from Vijender, Akhil and Jeetendra Kumar are also participating in the professional boxing competition to be held in April this year
 is pratiyogita main bharat ke dblubio asia papeefic middlawet champion vijender kaa saamana dablyubio oriental super midilwet championships or china ke mukkebaaz julpikar mematiyaali se hoga
 However, information about Akhil and Jeetendra's rivals will be given in the last week of March
 mumbai main ek april ko hone vaali is pratiyogita kii taiyaariyon ke bare main akhil ne kaha, "maine bahut acchhee taiyaari kar rakhi he or ab main puri tarah se taiyaar hum, bas ring main utarane kii deree he
 " haryana main police up adheekshak ke rup main seva de rahe akhil ko haal hi main haryana sarkaar se profeshnal boxing ke liye anumati mili he
 He is landing in the ring after a long time
 aise main kshamta kii kami ke bare main puche jane par akhil ne kaha, "mere paas anubhav he
 All i need is a good strategy and ios is preparing a good plan
 aashaa he ki ham ioes ke saath lambey samay tak khelen
 "comments rashtramandal khelon-2006 main swarna padak vijeta rahe akhil ne kai antarrashtriya pratiyogitaaon main desh kaa netritv kiya he
 Akhil, a bronze medalist in the 2008 Boxing World Cup, said that to win in any competition requires willpower
